RESUMO 

Esta pesquisa teve como objetivo geral compreender a abordagem sobre o ensino de fun√ß√µes 
exponenciais, associadas ao uso do GeoGebra, no Ensino M√©dio em produ√ß√µes cient√≠ficas, em 
livros  did√°ticos  e  em  tarefas  matem√°ticas.  Para  isso,  o  caminho  metodol√≥gico  do  estudo 
qualitativo compreendeu: a an√°lise das abordagens e discuss√µes sobre as fun√ß√µes exponenciais, 
associadas √† ferramenta GeoGebra, na literatura brasileira cient√≠fica mais recente; a an√°lise da 
abordagem  das  tarefas  e  suas  representa√ß√µes  sobre  este  conceito  em  livros  did√°ticos  de 
Matem√°tica voltados √† supracitada etapa da Educa√ß√£o B√°sica e, por fim, a an√°lise e proposi√ß√£o 
de uma abordagem envolvendo tarefas com fun√ß√µes exponenciais por meio do uso did√°tico do 
software GeoGebra para o citado n√≠vel escolar. Verificamos que, no meio cient√≠fico, o ensino 
de  fun√ß√µes  exponenciais  est√°  muito  associado  a  contextos  da  realidade,  de  modo  que  sua 
aplica√ß√£o como modelo de estudo de fen√¥menos f√≠sicos (termodin√¢mica), financeiros (juros) e 
biol√≥gicos (reprodu√ß√£o de bact√©rias) √© recorrente nas pesquisas filtradas. Al√©m disso, entre os 
estudos analisados,  h√° uma preocupa√ß√£o  comum em  permitir que os  estudantes estabele√ßam 
rela√ß√µes entre as representa√ß√µes semi√≥ticas deste tipo de fun√ß√£o matem√°tica, principalmente, a 
alg√©brica  e  a  gr√°fica.  Nesta  vertente,  a  principal  contribui√ß√£o  did√°tica,  proveniente  da 
associa√ß√£o  entre  as  fun√ß√µes  exponenciais  e  o  GeoGebra,  √©  o  car√°ter  experimental  que  este 
software imprime em sala de aula, permitindo que os estudantes desenvolvam sua autonomia, 
passando  a  perceber  rela√ß√µes  entre  diferentes  representa√ß√µes.  Verificamos  que  os  livros 
did√°ticos apresentam, exclusivamente, tarefas na forma de exerc√≠cios e problemas. Carecem, 
assim,  de tarefas de estrutura aberta, que permitam que os alunos experimentem,  durante as 
aulas de fun√ß√µes exponenciais, processos investigativos. Desta forma, poderiam exercitar sua 
capacidade  de  conjectura,  reflex√£o  e  descoberta  pela  experimenta√ß√£o,  em  vez  de  receber  e 
aplicar  defini√ß√µes  e  propriedades  prontas  e  de  forma  objetiva.  Entendemos  que  tal  car√°ter 
experimental pode ser alcan√ßado com aux√≠lio do GeoGebra, conforme apontam as pesquisas 
recentes e as tarefas propostas neste estudo. 

Palavras-chaves:  Fun√ß√£o  exponencial;  GeoGebra;  Produ√ß√µes  cient√≠ficas;  Livros  Did√°ticos; 
Tarefas Matem√°ticas.

 
 
ABSTRACT 

This research had as general objective to understand the approach on the teaching of exponential 
functions,  associated  with  the  use  of  GeoGebra,  in  high  school  in  scientific  productions,  in 
textbooks and in mathematical tasks. For this, the methodological path of the qualitative study 
included: the analysis of approaches and discussions on exponential functions, associated with 
the GeoGebra tool, in the most recent Brazilian scientific literature; the analysis of the approach 
to  tasks  and  their  representations  of  this  concept  in  Mathematics  textbooks  aimed  at  the 
aforementioned  stage  of  Basic  Education  and,  finally,  the  analysis  and  proposition  of  an 
approach  involving  tasks  with  exponential  functions  through  the  didactic  use  of  GeoGebra 
software for the aforementioned school level. We found that, in the scientific world, teaching 
of exponential functions is much associated with contexts of reality, so that its application as a 
model for the study of physical (thermodynamic), financial (interest) and biological (bacterial 
reproduction)  phenomena  is  recurrent  in  filtered  searches.  In  addition,  among  the  studies 
analyzed, there is a common concern in allowing students to establish relations between the 
semiotic representations of this type of mathematical function, mainly algebraic and graphical. 
In this aspect, the main didactic contribution, derived from the association between exponential 
functions and GeoGebra, is the experimental character that this software prints in the classroom, 
allowing students to develop their autonomy, starting to perceive relations between different 
representations.  We  verified  that  the  textbooks  present,  exclusively,  tasks  in  the  form  of 
exercises and problems. Thus, they lack tasks with an open structure, which allow students to 
experience, during classes of exponential functions, the investigative processes. In this way, 
they  could  exercise  their  capacity  for  conjecture,  reflection  and  discovery  through 
experimentation, instead of receiving and applying ready-made definitions and properties in an 
objective manner. We understand that such an experimental character can be achieved with the 
help of GeoGebra, as pointed out by recent research and the tasks proposed in this study. 

Keywords:  Exponential  function;  GeoGebra;  Scientific  productions;  Didatic  books;  Math 
Tasks.

CAP√çTULO I - ARTIGO 01 

FUN√á√ÉO  EXPONENCIAL  E  GEOGEBRA:  O  QUE  VEM  SENDO  DISCUTIDO  NA 
LITERATURA BRASILEIRA? 

RESUMO 

Esta pesquisa √© parte de uma disserta√ß√£o de mestrado e o objetivo √© foi investigar como a abordagem 
sobre  ensino  de  fun√ß√£o  exponencial  vinculado  ao  uso  do  GeoGebra  vem  sendo  discutida  em  artigos 
publicados entre os anos 2010 - 2019 em peri√≥dicos brasileiros da √°rea de Ensino, cujo escopo contenha 
o ensino de Matem√°tica e/ou de ci√™ncias. Este √© um trabalho qualitativo bibliogr√°fico e descritivo. Foi 
constatado  que  o  ensino  de  fun√ß√£o  exponencial  tem  sido  potencializado,  muito  por  conta  de  suas 
aplica√ß√µes em contexto de realidade (como na biologia e na matem√°tica financeira) que, associadas ao 
GeoGebra,  otimizam  a  aula  de  matem√°tica,  concedendo-a  um  car√°ter  experimental  que  estimula  a 
autonomia  dos  estudantes,  aos  lhes  permitir  construir  os  conceitos  por  meio  de  suas  m√∫ltiplas 
representa√ß√µes,  a  partir  da  supervis√£o  do  professor  que,  al√©m  de  mediador,  precisa  incorporar  e  ter 
dom√≠nio sobre o uso das Tecnologias de Informa√ß√£o e Comunica√ß√£o em sala de aula. 

Palavras-chave: Fun√ß√£o Exponencial; GeoGebra; Produ√ß√µes cient√≠ficas; 

ABSTRACT 

This research  is  part  of  a master's  thesis and  the  aim  is  to  investigate  how  the approach to  teaching 
exponential function linked to the use of GeoGebra has been discussed in articles published between 
2010  -  2019  in  Brazilian  journals  in  the  field  of  Education,  whose  scope  contains  the  teaching  of 
Mathematics and/or science. This is a qualitative bibliographic and descriptive work. It was found that 
the teaching of exponential function has been enhanced, largely because of its applications in the context 
of  reality  (as  in  biology  and  financial  mathematics)  which,  associated  with  GeoGebra,  optimize  the 
mathematics class, giving it an experimental character that encourages students' autonomy by allowing 
them to build concepts through their multiple representations, based on the supervision of the teacher 
who, in addition to being a mediator, needs to incorporate and have mastery over the use of Information 
and Communication Technologies in the classroom. 

Key-words: Exponential Function; GeoGebra; Scientific Productions.

Este artigo faz parte de uma disserta√ß√£o de mestrado estruturada em formato multipaper e tem como

Para  realizar  tal  an√°lise  nos  baseamos  na  classifica√ß√£o  de  tarefas  de  Ponte  (2005)  e  na  Teoria  dos 
Registros de Representa√ß√£o Semi√≥tica de Duval (2017). Esta √©, portanto, uma pesquisa explorat√≥ria, 
quanto  aos  seus  objetivos,  e  documental,  quanto  aos  procedimentos.  Como  principais  conclus√µes,

principalmente atrelados a objetivos de fixa√ß√£o e repeti√ß√£o, al√©m de problemas vinculados √†s aplica√ß√µes 
da fun√ß√£o exponencial, uma constante nas tr√™s obras. Verificamos tamb√©m uma  prioriza√ß√£o massiva

Palavras ‚Äì Chave:  Fun√ß√£o exponencial. Tarefas. Representa√ß√µes semi√≥ticas.  

Abstract 

This article is part of a master's thesis structured multipaper format and aims to investigate the types of 
mathematical  tasks,  as  well  as  the  semiotic  representations  involved  in  the  chapters  on  exponential 
function of three textbooks for the 1st year of high school selected distinct collections in the current 
PNLD (2016 ‚Äì 2020) by public schools in the city of Barreiras ‚Äì BA. To carry out such analysis, we 
based  on  the  classification  of  tasks  by  Ponte  (2005)  and  the  Theory  of  Records  of  Semiotic 
Representation of Duval (2017). This is, therefore, an exploratory research, in terms of its objectives, 
and documentary, in terms of procedures. As main conclusions, we note a strong tendency of textbooks 
to propose tasks of closed structure mainly linked to the objectives of fixation and repetition, in addition 
to problems related to the applications of the exponential function, a constant in the three works. We 
also verified a massive prioritization by algebraic representation, in addition to a majority of tasks that 
required  transition  between  records  with  the  privilege  to  congruent  senses.  We  recommend  the 
fundamentals of TRRS as a tool for selecting tasks for evaluations so that the evaluation process takes 
into account the phenomenon of congruence. 

Key words: Exponential function. Tasks. Semiotic representations

CAP√çTULO III ‚Äì ARTIGO 03 

FUN√á√ÉO EXPONENCIAL: UMA PROPOSI√á√ÉO DE TAREFAS MATEM√ÅTICAS 

RESUMO 

Este artigo faz parte de uma disserta√ß√£o de mestrado em formato multipaper cujo objetivo foi propor e 
analisar tarefas matem√°ticas, bem como suas representa√ß√µes semi√≥ticas, envolvendo as fun√ß√µes 
do tipo exponencial com o emprego do software GeoGebra. Para isso, nos ancoramos nos estudos 
sobre o conceito e classifica√ß√£o de tarefas de Ponte (2005) e na Teoria dos Registros de Representa√ß√£o 
Semi√≥tica  de  Duval  (2017).  Esta  √©  uma  pesquisa  qualitativa  (GERHARDT;  SILVEIRA,  2009)  e 
interpretativista  (DIVAN;  OLIVEIRA,  2008).  A  constru√ß√£o  das  propostas  passou  pela  elabora√ß√£o  e 
adapta√ß√£o  das  tarefas por meio  de  testagem  no  GeoGebra, seguida  pela  composi√ß√£o  das  orienta√ß√µes 
did√°ticas ao professor. Ressaltamos a import√¢ncia do trabalho em sala de aula seja marcado por uma 
diversifica√ß√£o de tipos de tarefas considerando o assunto a ser ensinado, as caracter√≠sticas dos alunos e 
as  compet√™ncias  e  habilidades  que  se  pretende  desenvolver.  O  software  GeoGebra  se  mostrou  um 
recurso did√°tico adequado para a proposi√ß√£o de tarefas sobre fun√ß√µes do tipo exponencial por possibilitar 
um car√°ter experimental √† aula, o que poder√° conceber ao aluno do ensino m√©dio a autonomia para testar 
hip√≥teses,  gerar  conjecturas,  analisar  simultaneamente  a  rela√ß√£o  entre  elementos  de  representa√ß√µes 
distintas e aprender pela descoberta e n√£o pela simples aceita√ß√£o te√≥rica.   

Palavras ‚Äì Chave:  Fun√ß√£o exponencial. GeoGebra. Tarefas. Representa√ß√µes semi√≥ticas.  

ABSTRACT 

This article is part of a master's thesis in multipaper format whose objective was to propose and analyze 
mathematical tasks, as well as their semiotic representations, involving exponential-type functions using 
GeoGebra software. For this, we anchored in studies on the concept and classification of tasks by Ponte 
(2005)  and  in  Duval's  Theory  of  Semiotic  Representation  Records  (2017).  This  is  a  qualitative 
(GERHARDT;  SILVEIRA,  2009)  and  interpretive  (DIVAN;  OLIVEIRA,  2008)  research.  The 
construction of the proposals went through the elaboration and adaptation of the tasks through testing in 
GeoGebra, followed by the composition of the didactic guidelines for the teacher. We emphasize the 
importance of work in the classroom being marked by a diversification of types of tasks considering the 
subject to be taught, the characteristics of the students and the skills and abilities to be developed. The 
GeoGebra software proved to be an adequate didactic resource for proposing tasks on exponential-type 
functions as it allows an experimental character to the class, which can give the high school student the 
autonomy  to  test  hypotheses,  generate  conjectures,  simultaneously  analyze  the  relationship  between 
elements  of  distinct  representations  and  learning  through  discovery  rather  than  mere  theoretical 
acceptance. 
Key words: Exponential function. GeoGebra. Tasks. Semiotic representations.

matem√°ticas,  bem  como  suas  representa√ß√µes  semi√≥ticas,  envolvendo  as  fun√ß√µes  do  tipo 

exponencial  com  o  emprego  do  software  GeoGebra.  Assim,  considerando  o  formato 

multipaper,  no  total,  foram  produzidos  tr√™s  artigos,  cada  um  correspondente  a  um  objetivo
